Very courteous staff. I usually just change my own oil, but was busy and took it here instead. When I walked in, the customer rep yelled out (something like) "New Customer" and all employees cheered. That was pretty cool.
All these type of "lube shops" always have suggestions beyond the standard oil change but the couple of times I've gone to a lube shop previously, they almost make you feel bad for not buying their recommendations. This is one of my favorite local shops! The owners are a kind couple, and they're always super welcoming to me and my son. They fry fresh fish, cut up huge jackfruits, and stock lots of chinese and other asian vegetables that my family loves. I will admit that some of the of their items are overpriced, but I'd rather support a local business than order a single ingredient online to get ship a million miles and get to me in a month. Also, many goods they have are usually hard to find in any other store, and I love being able to find them right across the street.</Review>

<user>106823100937098447497</user><username>Kyle Freeman< /username><date>1550038024865< /date><Rate>4< /Rate>< Review>
Hard to find initially but once you know where it is then it is fine. Has a distinct odor like it has been flooded.

There is a small selection of packing materials for purchase and the standard drop off slots you are accustomed to.

If there was any location that should stay open later it is this one, but sadly it does not. Several times I have tried coming here only to find a sign telling me it was closed and it had been in the middle of the day. Not sure why.

They were closed for a long time ostensibly for a remodel, but no noticeable change was made. No post office is kept up to date by any means and this one is no different. It isn't dirty, but it is a noticeable clash from coming right from Macy's. Granted, subjective in a way, but it is depressing going to any post office because of their choice of atmosphere it seems.

When I have been able to catch this one open I've been able to reliably complete my transactions. They seem to have knowledgeable staff that can process a line fairly quickly.

Conclusion being... Update this location and fix the odor issue. Not sure how Macy's welcomes the clash in decor. This location has great people and they should be rewarded with a better workplace.<//Review>

< text>
Hard to find, but full-service post office with 3-4 clerks.  Very friendly and efficient.  Enter Macy's (the main store, not the men's store) from Stockton, turn left through cosmetics, take the down escalator; turn right through Faberware (note picture).  Door is practically invisible. I walked into Teddy's Cafe many years ago on the 2nd day of his operation.  Religiously I have not stopped eating there in over 24+ years.  I don't know if anything else needs to be said.
